Question: An organization decided to raise Rs. 6 lakh by collecting equal contribution from each of its employees. If each of them had contributed Rs. 60 extra, the contribution would have been Rs. 6.24 lakh. How many employees are there in that organization?
Choices:
  A: 300
  B: 200
  C: 400
  D: 100
  E: 500
Response 0:
Let the number of employees in the organization be x.
Then, the amount contributed by each employee is 6,00,000/x.
If each employee had contributed Rs. 60 extra, the new contribution per employee would be (6,24,000/x).
According to the problem,
(6,24,000/x) = (6,00,000/x) + 60
Solving the above equation, we get:
x = 400
Therefore, there are 400 employees in the organization.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Let's assume that there are 'n' employees in the organization.
Knowledge:
  If each employee contributes 'x' amount, then the total contribution would be 'n*x'.
  The total contribution would be Rs. 6 lakh if each employee contributes equally.
  The total contribution would be Rs. 6.24 lakh if each employee contributes Rs. 60 extra.
  So, we can form the following two equations:
    n*x = 6,00,000  ---(1)
    n*(x+60) = 6,24,000 ---(2)

Action: 
  We can solve these equations to find the value of 'n'.
  Multiplying equation (1) by (x+60) and equation (2) by 'x', we get:
    n*x*(x+60) = 6,00,000*(x+60)  ---(3)
    n*x*(x+60) = 6,24,000*x     ---(4)
  Dividing equation (3) by equation (4), we get:
    (x+60)/x = 6,24,000/(6,00,000+60*6,24,000/x)
    (x+60)/x = 104/101
    Solving this equation, we get:
    x = 6000
  Substituting this value of 'x' in equation (1), we get:
    n = 6,00,000/6000 = 100
  Therefore, there are 100 employees in that organization.

Question: A man divides Rs 8600 among 5 sons, 4 daughters and 2 nephews. If each daughter receives four times as much as each nephew, and each son receives five as much as each nephew. How much does each daughter receive ?
Choices:
  A: Rs 400
  B: Rs 500
  C: Rs 600
  D: Rs 700
  E: Rs 800
Response 0:

Amount received by each daughter = 4x
Amount received by each son = 5x

Total number of children = 5 sons + 4 daughters + 2 nephews = 11
Total amount = Rs 8600

We can set up an equation based on the given information:
5(5x) + 4(4x) + 2(x) = 8600

Simplifying the equation:
25x + 16x + 2x = 8600
43x = 8600
x = 200

Therefore, each nephew receives Rs 200.
Each daughter receives 4x = 4(200) = Rs 800.

Question: A student instead of finding the value of 7/8 of a number, found the value of 7/18 of the number. If his answer differed from the actual one by 770, find the that number.
Choices:
  A: 1584
  B: 2520
  C: 1728
  D: 1656
  E: None
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let the number be x.
  The student found the value of 7/18 of the number, instead of 7/8 of the number.
  The student's answer was 770 less than the actual one.
  We can set up an equation to solve for x.
  Actual value - Student's value = 770
  (7/8)x - (7/18)x = 770
  We can simplify the equation by finding a common denominator.
  (63/72)x - (28/72)x = 770
  (35/72)x = 770
  x = (770*72)/35
Action: Answer("A")  
Therefore, the number is 1584.
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  Let the number be x.
  The student found the value of 7/18 of x instead of 7/8 of x.
  The difference between the actual value and the value found by the student is 770.
  We can use the formula: Error = Actual Value - Value found by the student.
  We can also use the formula: Error = (Fractional Error) x (Actual Value).
  Fractional Error = (Actual Value - Value found by the student) / Actual Value.

Calculation:
  Let the actual value be y.
  Fractional Error = (y - (7/18)x) / y = (7/8)
  Solving for y, we get y = (18/11)x.
  Error = Actual Value - Value found by the student = y - (7/18)x = (11/18)x.
  (11/18)x = 770
  x = (770 x 18) / 11 = 1260 x 2 = 2520

Question: Calculate the maximum distance you can travel with $8.50 on a cab which charges $3.50 for the first quarter-mile and 10 cents for each additional quarter mile.
Choices:
  A: 11.75 miles
  B: 12.75 miles
  C: 17.75 miles
  D: 14.75 miles
  E: 10.75 miles
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The cab charges $3.50 for the first quarter-mile and 10 cents for each additional quarter mile.
  
Calculation:
  Let's assume the maximum distance you can travel is D miles.
  The first quarter-mile costs $3.50, which means the remaining balance is $5.00 ($8.50 - $3.50).
  The cost of each additional quarter-mile is $0.10.
  Therefore, the number of additional quarter-miles you can travel is $5.00 / $0.10 = 50.
  The total distance you can travel is 0.25 + 50 * 0.25 = 12.75 miles.
  
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  The cab charges $3.50 for the first quarter-mile and 10 cents for each additional quarter mile.
  We need to find the maximum distance that can be traveled with $8.50.
  
Solution:
  Let's first calculate the cost of each additional quarter-mile:
  $0.10/quarter-mile
  Now, let's calculate how many quarter-miles can be traveled with the remaining $5.00:
  $5.00 / $0.10/quarter-mile = 50 quarter-miles
  The total distance traveled will be the sum of the first quarter-mile and the 50 additional quarter-miles:
  Total distance = 1 quarter-mile + 50 quarter-miles = 51 quarter-miles
  Finally, we need to convert quarter-miles to miles:
  51 quarter-miles * 0.25 miles/quarter-mile = 12.75 miles

  The first quarter-mile costs $3.50, and the remaining (4d - 1) quarter-miles cost (4d - 1) * $0.10 = $0.40d - $0.10.
  Therefore, we can write the following equation:
  $3.50 + $0.40d - $0.10 = $8.50
  Simplifying the equation, we have:
  $0.40d = $5.10
  d = $5.10 / $0.40
  d = 12.75 miles
